1.
Short title; reference; expired provisions
(a)
Short title
This Act may be cited as the
Miscellaneous Tariff Bill Act of 2017
.
(b)
Reference
Except as otherwise expressly provided, whenever in this Act an amendment or repeal is expressed in terms of an amendment to, or repeal of, a chapter, subchapter, note, additional U.S. note, heading, subheading, or other provision, the reference shall be considered to be made to a chapter, subchapter, note, additional U.S. note, heading, subheading, or other provision of the Harmonized Tariff Schedule of the United States.
(c)
Expired provisions
Subchapter II of chapter 99 is amendedâ
(1)
by striking heading 9902.01.01 and all headings that follow through the end of such subchapter; and
(2)
by striking U.S. Note 7 and U.S. Notes 13 through 19.

1677.
Effective date
The amendments made by this Act apply to goods entered, or withdrawn from warehouse for consumption, on or after the 30th day after the date of the enactment of this Act.
